(*****************************************************************

 Limits in enriched categories

 In this file, we define the notion of limit in enriched
 categories. Note that these limits refer to weighted limits
 rather than so-called conical limits, because the former is
 actually the correct notion of limit in this setting.

 Contents
 1. Cones of enriched limits
 2. Limits in an enriched category
 3. Being a limit is a proposition
 4. Some accessors for enriched limits
 5. Enriched limits are unique up to isomorphism
 6. Uniqueness of enriched limits
 7. Instances of limits
 7.1. Powers as limits
 7.2. Conical limits as limits

 *****************************************************************)

Section EnrichedLimit.
  Context {V : sym_mon_closed_cat}
          {I C : category}
          (E : enrichment C V)
          (D : I ⟶ C)
          (W : I ⟶ V).

  (** * 1. Cones of enriched limits *)
  Definition enriched_lim_cone
    : UU
    := ∑ (a : C),
       ∑ (fs : ∏ (i : I), W i --> E ⦃ a , D i ⦄),
       ∏ (i j : I)
         (f : i --> j),
       fs i · postcomp_arr E a (#D f)
       =
       #W f · fs j.

  Coercion ob_enriched_lim_cone
           (a : enriched_lim_cone)
    : C
    := pr1 a.

  Definition enriched_lim_cone_pr
             (a : enriched_lim_cone)
             (i : I)
    : W i --> E ⦃ a , D i ⦄
    := pr12 a i.

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
I, C: category
E: enrichment C V
D: I ⟶ C
W: I ⟶ V
a: enriched_lim_cone
i, j: I
f: I ⟦ i, j ⟧
enriched_lim_cone_pr a i · postcomp_arr E a (# D f) =
# W f · enriched_lim_cone_pr a j

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
I, C: category
E: enrichment C V
D: I ⟶ C
W: I ⟶ V
a: enriched_lim_cone
i, j: I
f: I ⟦ i, j ⟧
enriched_lim_cone_pr a i · postcomp_arr E a (# D f) =
# W f · enriched_lim_cone_pr a j

    exact (pr22 a i j f).
  Qed.

  Definition make_enriched_lim_cone
             (a : C)
             (fs : ∏ (i : I), W i --> E ⦃ a , D i ⦄)
             (eqs : ∏ (i j : I)
                      (f : i --> j),
                    fs i · postcomp_arr E a (#D f)
                    =
                    #W f · fs j)
    : enriched_lim_cone
    := a ,, fs ,, eqs.

  (identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ enriched_lim_cone_pr a i
   · sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (E ⦃ a, D i ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E w a (D i))
· internal_pre_post_comp (# W (identity i))

  (identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ enriched_lim_cone_pr a j
   · sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (E ⦃ a, D j ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E w a (D j))
· internal_pre_post_comp (# W g)
    (postcomp_arr E w (# D (identity j)))

   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (E ⦃ a, D j ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E w a (D j))) #⊗ h
· (internal_lam
     (identity (W j ⊸ (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄)) #⊗ # W g
      · internal_eval (W j) (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄)
      · identity (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄)) #⊗ identity (W i)
   · internal_eval (W i) (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄))

· (identity (W i ⊸ (E ⦃ w, D i ⦄)) #⊗ identity (W i)
   · internal_eval (W i) (E ⦃ w, D i ⦄)
   · postcomp_arr E w (# D g)) =
internal_lam
  (identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ enriched_lim_cone_pr a j
   · (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (E ⦃ a, D j ⦄)
      · enriched_comp E w a (D j))) #⊗ h
· (identity (W j ⊸ (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄)) #⊗ # W g
   · internal_eval (W j) (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄)
   · identity (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄))

    · sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (E ⦃ a, D j ⦄)
    · enriched_comp E w a (D j))
 · identity (W j ⊸ (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄))) #⊗ (h · # W g)
· internal_eval (W j) (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄) =
identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ h
· identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ # W g
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (W j)
· enriched_lim_cone_pr a j #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄)
· enriched_comp E w a (D j)

w: C

z: V
h: V ⟦ z, W i ⟧
internal_lam
  (identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ enriched_lim_cone_pr a j
   · sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (E ⦃ a, D j ⦄)
   · enriched_comp E w a (D j)) #⊗ (h · # W g)
· internal_eval (W j) (E ⦃ w, D j ⦄) =
identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ h
· identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) #⊗ # W g
· sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) (W j)

· enriched_comp E w a (D j)

  Defined.

  Definition is_lim_enriched
             (a : enriched_lim_cone)
    : UU
    := ∏ (w : C),
       is_end (weighted_hom w) (is_lim_enriched_wedge a w).

  Definition lim_enriched
    : UU
    := ∑ (a : enriched_lim_cone),
       is_lim_enriched a.

  Coercion cone_of_lim_enriched
           (a : lim_enriched)
    : enriched_lim_cone
    := pr1 a.

  Definition enriched_lim_cone_is_lim
             (a : lim_enriched)
    : is_lim_enriched a
    := pr2 a.

  (** * 3. Being a limit is a proposition * *)
  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat

E: enrichment C V
D: I ⟶ C
W: I ⟶ V
a: enriched_lim_cone
isaprop (is_lim_enriched a)

I, C: category

D: I ⟶ C

a: enriched_lim_cone
isaprop (is_lim_enriched a)

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
I, C: category
E: enrichment C V
D: I ⟶ C
W: I ⟶ V
a: enriched_lim_cone
t: C
t0: wedge (weighted_hom t)
isofhlevel 1
  ((λ t0 : wedge (weighted_hom t),
    iscontr
      (wedge_map (weighted_hom t) t0
         (is_lim_enriched_wedge a t))) t0)

    apply isapropiscontr.
  Qed.

  (** * 4. Some accessors for enriched limits *)
  Section LimMap.
    Context (a : lim_enriched)
            {x : C}
            (fs : ∏ (i : I), I_{ V} --> W i ⊸ (E ⦃ x, D i ⦄))
            (ps : ∏ (i j : I)
                    (g : i --> j),
                  fs i
                  · internal_pre_post_comp (identity (W i)) (postcomp_arr E x (# D g))
                  =
                  fs j
                  · internal_pre_post_comp (# W g) (postcomp_arr E x (identity (D j)))).

    (postcomp_arr E x (# D g)) =
fs j
· internal_pre_post_comp (# W g)
    (postcomp_arr E x (identity (D j)))
is_wedge (weighted_hom x)
  (make_wedge_data (weighted_hom x) I_{ V} fs)

    Definition mor_from_lim_enriched
      : x --> a
      := enriched_to_arr
           E
           (mor_to_end'
              _
              (enriched_lim_cone_is_lim a x)
              I_{V}
              fs
              mor_from_lim_enriched_wedge).

· internal_pre_post_comp (# W g)
    (postcomp_arr E x (identity (D j)))
i: I
q:= mor_to_end'_comm (weighted_hom x)
  (enriched_lim_cone_is_lim a x) I_{ V} fs
  mor_from_lim_enriched_wedge i: mor_to_end' (weighted_hom x)
  (enriched_lim_cone_is_lim a x) I_{ V} fs
  mor_from_lim_enriched_wedge
· mor_of_wedge (weighted_hom x)
    (is_lim_enriched_wedge a x) i = fs i
enriched_lim_cone_pr a i
· (mon_rinvunitor (E ⦃ a, D i ⦄)
   · identity (E ⦃ a, D i ⦄)
     #⊗ mor_to_end' (weighted_hom x)
          (enriched_lim_cone_is_lim a x) I_{ V} fs
          mor_from_lim_enriched_wedge
   · enriched_comp E x a (D i)) =
mon_linvunitor (W i) · fs i #⊗ identity (W i)
· internal_eval (W i) (E ⦃ x, D i ⦄)

         · (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x, a ⦄)
              (E ⦃ a, D i ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E x a (D i)))
      #⊗ identity (W i)
      · internal_eval (W i) (E ⦃ x, D i ⦄))) =
identity I_{ V} #⊗ h
· (enriched_from_arr E g #⊗ identity (W i)
   · (internal_lam
        (identity (E ⦃ x, a ⦄)
         #⊗ enriched_lim_cone_pr a i
         · (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x, a ⦄)
              (E ⦃ a, D i ⦄)
            · enriched_comp E x a (D i)))
      #⊗ identity (W i)
      · internal_eval (W i) (E ⦃ x, D i ⦄)))

      
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
I, C: category
E: enrichment C V
D: I ⟶ C
W: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched
x: C
f, g: C ⟦ x, a ⟧
p: ∏ i : I,
enriched_lim_cone_pr a i #⊗ enriched_from_arr E f
· enriched_comp E x a (D i) =
enriched_lim_cone_pr a i #⊗ enriched_from_arr E g
· enriched_comp E x a (D i)
i: I
z: V
h: V ⟦ z, W i ⟧
enriched_from_arr E f #⊗ identity (W i)
· (internal_lam
     (identity (E ⦃ x, a ⦄)
      #⊗ enriched_lim_cone_pr a i
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x, a ⦄)
           (E ⦃ a, D i ⦄) · enriched_comp E x a (D i)))
   #⊗ identity (W i)
   · internal_eval (W i) (E ⦃ x, D i ⦄)) =
enriched_from_arr E g #⊗ identity (W i)
· (internal_lam
     (identity (E ⦃ x, a ⦄)
      #⊗ enriched_lim_cone_pr a i
      · (sym_mon_braiding V (E ⦃ x, a ⦄)
           (E ⦃ a, D i ⦄) · enriched_comp E x a (D i)))
   #⊗ identity (W i)
   · internal_eval (W i) (E ⦃ x, D i ⦄))

· enriched_comp E x a (D i)

      exact (p i).
    Qed.
  End LimUnique.

  (** * 5. Enriched limits are unique up to isomorphism *)
  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
I, C: category
E: enrichment C V
D: I ⟶ C
W: I ⟶ V
a₁, a₂: lim_enriched
i, j: I
g: I ⟦ i, j ⟧
internal_lam
  (mon_lunitor (W i) · enriched_lim_cone_pr a₁ i)
· internal_pre_post_comp (identity (W i))
    (postcomp_arr E a₁ (# D g)) =
internal_lam
  (mon_lunitor (W j) · enriched_lim_cone_pr a₁ j)
· internal_pre_post_comp (# W g)
    (postcomp_arr E a₁ (identity (D j)))

H: is_univalent C
a₁, a₂: enriched_lim_cone
q: z_iso a₁ a₂
r: ∏ i : I,
enriched_lim_cone_pr a₁ i =
enriched_lim_cone_pr a₂ i · precomp_arr E (D i) q
a₁ = a₂
 exact (isotoid C H q).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
I, C: category
E: enrichment C V
D: I ⟶ C
W: I ⟶ V
H: is_univalent C
a₁, a₂: enriched_lim_cone
q: z_iso a₁ a₂
r: ∏ i : I,
enriched_lim_cone_pr a₁ i =
enriched_lim_cone_pr a₂ i · precomp_arr E (D i) q
∏ i : I,
enriched_lim_cone_pr a₁ i =
enriched_lim_cone_pr a₂ i
· precomp_arr E (D i) (idtoiso (isotoid C H q))

∏ i : I,

      exact r.
  Qed.

· internal_eval (W (pr1 (i,, i)))

mor_of_wedge (weighted_hom E D W w)
  (is_lim_enriched_wedge E D W (pr1 a) w) i #⊗ h
· internal_eval (W (pr1 (i,, i)))
    (E ⦃ w, D (pr2 (i,, i)) ⦄)

(** * 7.2. Conical limits as limits *)
Section LimitToConical.
  Context {V : sym_mon_closed_cat}
          {C : category}
          (E : enrichment C V)
          {I : category}
          (D : I ⟶ C).

  Let W : I ⟶ V := constant_functor _ _ I_{V}.

  Context (a : lim_enriched E D W).

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
enriched_conical_lim_cone D

  
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
enriched_conical_lim_cone D

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
C
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
∏ i : I, C ⟦ ?a, D i ⟧
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
∏ (i j : I) (f : I ⟦ i, j ⟧), ?ps i · # D f = ?ps j

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C

a: lim_enriched E D W
C
 exact a.
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
∏ i : I, C ⟦ a, D i ⟧
 exact (λ i, enriched_to_arr E (enriched_lim_cone_pr _ _ _ a i)).
    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
∏ (i j : I) (f : I ⟦ i, j ⟧),
(λ i0 : I,
 enriched_to_arr E (enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W a i0))
  i · # D f =
(λ i0 : I,
 enriched_to_arr E (enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W a i0))
  j
 abstract
        (intros i j f ; cbn ;
         use (invmaponpathsweq (make_weq _ (isweq_enriched_from_arr E _ _))) ; cbn ;
         rewrite enriched_from_to_arr ;
         pose (enriched_lim_cone_commute _ _ _ a f) as p ;
         cbn in p ;
         rewrite id_left in p ;
         rewrite <- p ;
         rewrite enriched_from_arr_comp ;
         rewrite enriched_from_to_arr ;
         rewrite tensor_split ;
         rewrite !assoc ;
         rewrite <- tensor_linvunitor ;
         rewrite !assoc' ;
         apply maponpaths ;
         rewrite !assoc ;
         apply idpath).
  Defined.

  Section ConicalLimUMP.
    Context {w : C}
            (v : V)
            (fs : ∏ (i : I), v --> E ⦃ w, D i ⦄)
            (ps : ∏ (i j : I) (k : i --> j), fs i · postcomp_arr E w (#D k) = fs j).

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
w: C
v: V
fs: ∏ i : I, V ⟦ v, E ⦃ w, D i ⦄ ⟧
ps: ∏ (i j : I) (k : I ⟦ i, j ⟧),
fs i · postcomp_arr E w (# D k) = fs j
isaprop
  (∑ g : V ⟦ v, E ⦃ w, a ⦄ ⟧,
   ∏ i : I,
   g
   · postcomp_arr E w
       (enriched_to_arr E
          (enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W a i)) = fs i)

    
V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
w: C
v: V
fs: ∏ i : I, V ⟦ v, E ⦃ w, D i ⦄ ⟧
ps: ∏ (i j : I) (k : I ⟦ i, j ⟧),
fs i · postcomp_arr E w (# D k) = fs j
isaprop
  (∑ g : V ⟦ v, E ⦃ w, a ⦄ ⟧,

   #⊗ pr1 φ₂ · enriched_comp E w (pr1 a) (D i))

V: sym_mon_closed_cat
C: category
E: enrichment C V
I: category
D: I ⟶ C
W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
w: C
v: V
fs: ∏ i : I, V ⟦ v, E ⦃ w, D i ⦄ ⟧
ps: ∏ (i j : I) (k : I ⟦ i, j ⟧),
fs i · postcomp_arr E w (# D k) = fs j
φ₁, φ₂: ∑ g : V ⟦ v, E ⦃ w, a ⦄ ⟧,
∏ i : I,
g
· postcomp_arr E w
    (enriched_to_arr E
       (enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W a i)) = fs i
i: I
z: V
h: V ⟦ z, I_{ V} ⟧
p: enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W a i #⊗ pr1 φ₁
· enriched_comp E w a (D i) =
enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W a i #⊗ pr1 φ₂
· enriched_comp E w a (D i)
enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W (pr1 a) i #⊗ pr1 φ₁
· enriched_comp E w (pr1 a) (D i) =
enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W (pr1 a) i #⊗ pr1 φ₂
· enriched_comp E w (pr1 a) (D i)

      exact p.
    Qed.

W:= constant_functor I V I_{ V}: I ⟶ V
a: lim_enriched E D W
w: C
v: V
fs: ∏ i : I, V ⟦ v, E ⦃ w, D i ⦄ ⟧
ps: ∏ (i j : I) (k : I ⟦ i, j ⟧),
fs i · postcomp_arr E w (# D k) = fs j
i, j: I
f: I ⟦ i, j ⟧
z: V
h: V ⟦ z, I_{ V} ⟧
fs i · postcomp_arr E w (# D f) = fs j

      apply ps.
    Qed.

   · internal_eval (W (pr1 (i,, i)))
       (E ⦃ w, D (pr2 (i,, i)) ⦄))

i: I
p: sym_mon_braiding V v I_{ V}
· enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W (pr1 a) i
  #⊗ mor_to_end (weighted_hom E D W w) (pr2 a w)
       enriched_weighted_to_conical_is_conical_lim_wedge
· enriched_comp E w (pr1 a) (D i) =
mon_runitor v · fs i
enriched_weighted_to_conical_is_conical_lim_mor
· mon_linvunitor (E ⦃ w, a ⦄)
· enriched_from_arr E
    (enriched_to_arr E
       (enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W a i))
  #⊗ identity (E ⦃ w, a ⦄) =
mon_rinvunitor v · sym_mon_braiding V v I_{ V}
· enriched_lim_cone_pr E D W (pr1 a) i
  #⊗ mor_to_end (weighted_hom E D W w) (pr2 a w)
       enriched_weighted_to_conical_is_conical_lim_wedge

  (is_conical_lim_enriched_diagram E D
     enriched_weighted_to_conical_cone w) v
i: Diagrams.vertex
  (Diagrams.graph_from_precategory I)
enriched_weighted_to_conical_is_conical_lim_mor v
  (pr1 cc) (pr2 cc)
· Graphs.Limits.coneOut
    (is_conical_lim_enriched_cone E D
       enriched_weighted_to_conical_cone w) i =
Graphs.Limits.coneOut cc i

      exact (enriched_weighted_to_conical_is_conical_lim_mor_eq v (pr1 cc) (pr2 cc) i).
